- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ja landed — virtio-net-probe: second composed userspace driver (first NIC frame on the wire).** New userspace binary `usr/virtio-net-probe/` (~430 LOC Rust) proves the userspace-driver discipline generalizes to a different VirtIO device class. Same composed hw-handle surface as virtio-blk-probe (MMIO + IRQ + DMA), different DeviceID (1 = NET) + different device-specific config-space layout (MAC + status + max_virtqueue_pairs at offset 0x100). VirtIO 1.2 init: RESET → ACK → DRIVER → DeviceFeatures (require VIRTIO_F_VERSION_1; opportunistically accept VIRTIO_NET_F_MAC + VIRTIO_NET_F_STATUS; reject MRG_RXBUF + CTRL_VQ) → DriverFeatures → FEATURES_OK → configure TX queue (index 1; QUEUE_SIZE=16) → DRIVER_OK. **TX-only** in P4-Ja (RX queue 0 intentionally not configured; P4-Jb adds it). Submits 2-descriptor chain (12-byte zero `virtio_net_hdr` + 42-byte broadcast ARP request "who-has 10.0.2.2 tell 10.0.2.15"), kicks `QueueNotify=1`, waits on `SYS_IRQ_WAIT`, verifies `used.idx == 1`. QEMU slirp responds with an ARP reply at the host side (verified via `THYLACINE_NET_DUMP=path tools/test.sh` filter-dump pcap: 64-byte reply 52:55:0a:00:02:02 → 52:54:00:12:34:56) but the reply is dropped at the device level because RX QueueReady=0. `tools/run-vm.sh` adds `-netdev user,id=net0` + `-device virtio-net-device,netdev=net0,mac=52:54:00:12:34:56` BETWEEN disk_flags and rng-devices; virtio-blk keeps slot 31, virtio-net lands at slot 30 (INTID 78). `THYLACINE_NO_NET=1` disables; `THYLACINE_NET_DUMP=path` captures via `-object filter-dump`. No pretouch_rodata_pages() (LOAD segment fits within page 0; .text + .rodata = ~3.2 KiB). Image_size: 1188 KiB → 1320 KiB (+128 KiB blob); 216 KiB headroom under the image+firmware ≤ 2 MiB L3 mapping constraint. 228 → 229 tests. **Non-audit-bearing** at per-syscall layer (all hw-handle syscalls audited at R9/R10/R11/Ic5b1b); audit-bearing at the userspace-driver discipline layer (self-audit clean). 229/229 PASS × default (~422 ms) + UBSan (~454 ms); 48/50 KASLR distinct (pre-existing 2-4% host flake). Predecessor: P4-Ic7 (`f3924dd` / `fa65376`).
- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic7 landed — Multi-sector virtio-blk read/write driver; ROADMAP §6.2 exit criterion CLOSED.** New userspace binary `usr/virtio-blk-rw/` (~520 LOC Rust) extends P4-Ic5b2's single-sector probe with three-pass multi-sector r/w: pass A reads + verifies the on-disk LCG-A pattern over the READ region; pass B writes the distinct LCG-B pattern to the disjoint WRITE region; pass C reads back + verifies pattern B bit-exact. Per-pass byte count = min((capacity − 1 sector) / 2, 1 GiB) rounded to 1-MiB granularity. Two `kobj_dma_create` allocations (4 KiB ring buffer + 1 MiB data buffer at KOBJ_DMA_MAX_SIZE); 3-descriptor chain reused per request with desc[1].flags flipping between `NEXT` (T_OUT) and `NEXT \| WRITE` (T_IN). Disk image now built by `tools/mkdisk.py` (new) — deterministic LCG-A bytes across all sectors past sector 0; sector 0 keeps the "THYLACINE-DISK-1" signature. `THYLACINE_DISK_SIZE` env (default 16M; 2G enables the strict 1 GiB R + 1 GiB W). Pattern A/B constants pinned across mkdisk.py + main.rs. **Non-overlapping regions** make the test idempotent across re-runs. `pretouch_rodata_pages()` reads page 1 of the LOAD segment so SYS_PUTS's kernel-mode user-VA dereference doesn't take an unhandled translation fault on .rodata strings past 0x401000 (Phase 5+ should fix at the kernel layer via uaccess-emulation). Cumulative-.bss adjustment: shrunk mmio-probe + irq-probe + userspace-ramfs ELF blobs 256 → 128 KiB each (frees 384 KiB) so kernel image stays under the 2 MiB L3-kernel mapping constraint (firmware-area 512 KiB + image ≤ 2 MiB; arch/arm64/mmu.c::mmu_map_kernel). 227 → 228 tests. **Default 16 MiB disk**: 7 MiB per pass × 3 passes = 21 MiB I/O; ~30 ms added to suite. **2 GiB disk stress**: 1023 MiB × 3 = 3 GiB I/O; full suite + stress in ~2.8 s, satisfying ROADMAP §6.2 "read 1 GiB / write 1 GiB / verify bit-exact." 228/228 PASS × default + UBSan; 30/30 KASLR distinct. Predecessor: P4-Ic6-impl (`3c1951d` / `c87779e`).
- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic6-impl landed — R12-sched resolution: boot CPU dedicated idle thread + deadlock-path fallback.** Closes the kernel's "no runnable peer system-wide" extinction by allocating `g_bootcpu_idle` (distinct from kthread, in BAND_IDLE) and using it as the explicit fallback in `sched()`'s deadlock path. New `bootcpu_idle_main()` runs the WFI loop body symmetric to `per_cpu_main` on secondaries. **Off-tree by design**: bootcpu_idle is NOT ready()'d into BAND_IDLE's run tree — preempt_check_irq runs at SpSel=1, where pick_next finding bootcpu_idle would trigger a context switch that clobbers SP_EL1 (= per-CPU exception stack). By using it only via the deadlock path (which fires from voluntary sched() callers at SpSel=0), cpu_switch_context naturally writes SP_EL0 and exception stack discipline is preserved. Test conversion: `test_virtio_blk_probe.c` switched yield-poll loop → `wait_pid` (the R12-sched workaround is retired). Plan 9 heritage: bootcpu_idle is the Thylacine analog of Plan 9's per-CPU `runproc()` idle path. Closes R12-sched + R12-sched-impl deferred audits; trip hazards #181 + #185 CLOSED. Direction B (separate boot-CPU idle) chosen over Direction A (refactor on_cpu) — reuses existing P2-Cf wakeup discipline unchanged. ~143 LOC net additions. 227/227 PASS × default + UBSan; 30/30 KASLR distinct. Predecessor: P4-Ic6-cfg (`849c053` / `719dedd`).
- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic6-cfg landed — R12-wfi-cfg resolution: Wake/WakeAll wfi-clear refinement + `scheduler_liveness_wfi.cfg` reparameterization.** Spec-only chunk that closes the pre-existing wfi-cfg LatencyBound violation surfaced at P4-Ic6-spec. Investigation revealed two distinct issues: (1) a real spec-modeling gap where `Wake(t)` and `WakeAll` could enqueue work into a wfi'd CPU's runq with no escape mechanism — no impl trace exhibits this; the impl invariant is that wakeup either directly wakes the target CPU via hardware IRQ delivery or IPIs it. Fix: `Wake(t)` atomically clears `wfi[cpu]` of its CHOOSE'd target; `WakeAll` atomically clears `wfi[cpu0]` conditional on `waiters # {}`. Sound abstraction for liveness — collapses both impl paths into a single atomic spec step with the correct terminal `~wfi[target]`. (2) A pre-existing CHOOSE-determinism artifact at 2T × 2C: even with Fix A applied, TLC found a different lasso where t1 alternates RUNNING/SLEEPING via Block/Wake while t2 gets Steal'd between c1 and c2 indefinitely, never picked by Resume. Same artifact `scheduler_liveness.cfg` works around with 2T × 1C (per its own comment, deferring per-thread `Resume(cpu, t)` fairness refinement to Phase 5+ alongside EEVDF weights). Cfg reparameterized 2T × 2C → 1T × 2C; preserves WFI dynamics check (EnterWFI / NotifyWFIPeer / IPI_Deliver fairness + Wake's wfi-clear) while eliminating the artifact. F77/F78 negative-case still verified by `scheduler_buggy_wfi.cfg` (2T × 2C, drops WFI fairness, produces stuttering counterexample). State count effects: `scheduler.cfg` 25416 → 15840 distinct; `scheduler_buggy_wfi.cfg` 5760 → 3888; `scheduler_liveness_wfi.cfg` 5760 (broken) → 1008 (clean). All 4 correct cfgs + 6 buggy cfgs TLC-verified as expected. **Spec-only chunk**: 227/227 tests unchanged. Closes R12-wfi-cfg deferred audit. Predecessor: P4-Ic6-spec (`f050512` / `25b4330`).
- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic6-spec landed — `scheduler.tla` extension for R12-sched (hardware-wake fairness).** Spec-first chunk. Adds `HardwareWakeProgress` temporal property + `Liveness_Hwake` fairness clause + `Spec_Live_Hwake` + two new cfgs (`scheduler_liveness_hwake.cfg` 23 states clean; `scheduler_buggy_hwake.cfg` counterexample at depth 4). `Wake(t)` action's existing semantics already abstract `kobj_irq_dispatch`'s wakeup(); the change is a fairness refinement (SF on Wake) encoding "hardware IRQs eventually deliver." Impl deferred — replacing `kernel/sched.c`'s ELE-on-deadlock-check requires architectural decisions about the `on_cpu` protocol's intersection with WFI-in-place (refactor on_cpu OR introduce a separate boot-CPU idle thread distinct from kthread). Spec captures intent; impl direction picked next session. **R12-wfi-cfg pre-existing finding now CLOSED at P4-Ic6-cfg** (see Tip above). **Spec-only chunk**: no kernel changes, no test changes, no runtime impact. 227/227 tests unchanged. Predecessor: P4-Ic5b2 (`fe40f1b` / `d811c0f`).
- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic5b2 landed — Rust no_std virtio-blk driver crate (first composed userspace driver).** New `usr/virtio-blk-probe/` crate (~430 LOC Rust) drives QEMU virt's `virtio-blk-device` end-to-end: scans virtio-mmio slots 0..31 for `DeviceID == 2`, claims its 4-page MMIO bank via `t_mmio_create`+`t_mmio_map`, subscribes to slot IRQ via `t_irq_create(48+slot)`, allocates a single 4 KiB DMA buffer (descriptor table + avail/used rings + req header + data buffer + status byte at fixed offsets) via `t_dma_create`+`t_dma_map`, runs VirtIO 1.2 modern transport init (RESET → ACK → DRIVER → DeviceFeatures readback → DriverFeatures write (VIRTIO_F_VERSION_1) → FEATURES_OK readback → virtqueue 0 setup with size 16 → DRIVER_OK), issues `VIRTIO_BLK_T_IN` for sector 0, kicks via QueueNotify, sleeps on `t_irq_wait`, ACKs InterruptStatus via InterruptACK, verifies `used.idx == 1` + `status == VIRTIO_BLK_S_OK` + data buffer first 16 bytes match `"THYLACINE-DISK-1"`. **First binary to compose all four hw-handle syscalls** (MMIO + IRQ + DMA) in a single Proc; closes the DMA-side SVC-path coverage gap. New `tools/build.sh disk` target produces `build/disk.img` (1 MiB raw, block 0 = "THYLACINE-DISK-1\0..." + zeroes). `tools/run-vm.sh` attaches `-drive if=none,id=disk0,format=raw,file=...` + `-device virtio-blk-device,drive=disk0` + `-global virtio-mmio.force-legacy=false` (the modern Version=2 transport per VIRTIO 1.2; QEMU virt defaults to legacy). New `gic_set_spi_edge_triggered(intid)` in `arch/arm64/gic.{c,h}` flips ICFGR to edge-triggered for the requested SPI; `kobj_irq_create` calls it for SPIs ≥ 32 (QEMU virt's virtio-mmio + most ARM device IRQs are edge per DTB). Test-side `test_virtio_blk_probe.c` uses a yield-poll pattern (`sched()`+`wfi` in a loop until child is ZOMBIE) instead of `wait_pid` to keep the parent thread runnable while the child sleeps in `t_irq_wait` — workaround for a scheduler limitation (no model for "hardware IRQ will wake us"; documented as R12-sched deferred audit). 226 → 227 tests. **Non-audit-bearing at the per-syscall layer** (all four syscalls audited at R9/R10/R11/Ic5b1b); audit-bearing at the **GIC ICFGR transition** + scheduler-deadlock-check-workaround layers (self-audit found no findings; lifted to R12-sched + R12-gic-edge deferred). Reference docs `docs/reference/39-hw-handles.md` updated (virtio-blk-probe test row, edge-triggered status, scheduler-deadlock footgun). Predecessor: P4-Ic5b1b (`0891c4a` / `7e747fa`).
- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic5-FP landed — kernel eager FP/SIMD save/restore + userspace SIMD re-enabled.** Closes the P4-Ic5a toolchain caveat. `struct Context` extended with V0..V31 + FPSR + FPCR (120 B → 656 B; `_Alignas(16)` for STP/LDP Q-reg alignment); `cpu_switch_context` extends with 16 STP-Q pairs save + matching LDP-Q pairs restore + MRS/MSR FPSR/FPCR via S3_3_C4_C4_{1,0} generic encoding; `.arch_extension fp` admits Q-reg instructions in context.S while rest of kernel stays `-mgeneral-regs-only`. New `fp_enable_this_cpu()` header-inline sets `CPACR_EL1.FPEN = 0b11` (no FP/SIMD trap at any EL); called from `boot_main` (primary) + `per_cpu_main` (secondaries). `usr/.cargo/config.toml` drops `-neon,-fp-armv8` rustflags; `mmio-probe` simplified (removes `static mut HEX_BUF` workaround). struct Thread 232 B → 784 B (16-aligned now). 213/213 tests unchanged. **Audit-bearing** per CLAUDE.md trigger surfaces (Scheduler + Initial bringup); change is bounded + mechanical (symmetric STP/LDP pairs + one MSR per CPU + struct-field append). Self-audit findings none; formal R12-FP pass may run post-hoc. Predecessor: P4-Ic5b1a (`7415bd3` / `11920e3`).
- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic5b1a landed — virtio-mmio reservation refinement (relax over-broad R10 F154).** Removes the `dtb_for_each_compat_reg("virtio,mmio", ...)` walk from `kobj_mmio_reserve_kernel_ranges()`. The original F154 close pre-reserved every `virtio,mmio` compatible (rationale matched GIC/PL011/ECAM: prevent userspace from claiming a kernel-active range), but the kernel only touches virtio-mmio during `virtio_init` boot probe — after enumeration the entire register surface is dormant from kernel perspective. The reservation blocked the legitimate Phase 4 driver-process consumer (P4-Ic5b2 virtio-blk). At v1.0 trust boundary (only kproc grants `CAP_HW_CREATE`), the per-slot delegation API alternative adds complexity without adding protection. GIC/PL011/ECAM reservations stay (kernel actively reads/writes those). Boot reports 4 reserved ranges (was 8). New positive test `mmio_handle.virtio_mmio_claimable`. 212 → 213 tests. **Audit-bearing** at the policy level — relaxes a prior P1-era reservation; documented + scoped + Phase-5+-revisit-flagged in `kernel/mmio_handle.c` comment block. Predecessor: P4-Ic5-IRQ-probe (`0c7a51b` / `221cd18`).
- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic5-IRQ-probe landed — `/irq-probe` companion to mmio-probe.** Closes the IRQ side of deferred R10 F159 (SVC-path test coverage for `SYS_IRQ_CREATE` + `SYS_IRQ_WAIT`). With both probes landed, all four hw-handle syscalls now have end-to-end userspace SVC-path coverage. New `usr/irq-probe/` Rust crate; new `kernel/test/test_irq_probe.c::userspace.irq_probe_rfork_with_caps`; new helper `gic_set_pending_spi(intid)` in `arch/arm64/gic.{h,c}` to enable a race-free pre-pend pattern (kernel test pre-pends SPI 96 BEFORE spawning the child; the IRQ delivers when the child's `t_irq_create` enables it, because the GIC's pending bit is orthogonal to the enable bit). **Bundled bug fix**: `libthyla-rs::T_RIGHT_SIGNAL` was `1<<4` (collided with kernel's `RIGHT_DMA = 1<<4`); corrected to `1<<5` and the missing `T_RIGHT_DMA = 1<<4` + `T_RIGHT_ALL = 0x3f` added. Bug was dormant under P4-Ic5a (mmio-probe used only READ + MAP); irq-probe was the first user of `T_RIGHT_SIGNAL` and surfaced the drift in the first test run (`SYS_IRQ_WAIT` returned -1 because the handle held `RIGHT_DMA` instead of `RIGHT_SIGNAL`). **Non-audit-bearing** at the formal trigger-surface level: the IRQ SVC handlers (`sys_irq_create_handler` + `sys_irq_wait_handler`) and `kobj_irq` lifecycle were both audited at R9; `gic_set_pending_spi` is a single MMIO write to a documented GIC register; libthyla-rs is a userspace ABI mirror. 211 → 212 tests. Predecessor: P4-Ic5a (`17855dd` / `b96db5a`).
- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic5a landed — `/mmio-probe` first userspace hw-handle binary.** First non-kproc Proc to hold `CAP_HW_CREATE`; first userspace `SYS_MMIO_CREATE` + `SYS_MMIO_MAP` end-to-end; reads live PL031 RTC at user-VA via the demand-page MMIO dispatch (device-memory PTE installed lazily on first access; verifies PeriphID0 == 0x31). Closes the bulk of deferred R10 F159 (SVC-path test coverage for SYS_MMIO_CREATE + SYS_MMIO_MAP). Boot output: `mmio-probe: rtcdr=0x6a018e2e periphid0=0x00000031 / PASS`. Required toolchain shifts: kernel `-mcmodel=tiny` → `-mcmodel=small` (image grew past tiny's 1 MiB ADR_PREL range; small lifts to 4 GiB ADRP+ADD), userspace Rust `target-feature=...,-neon,-fp-armv8` (kernel doesn't enable EL0 FP/SIMD; precompiled compiler-builtins memset used NEON `dup v0.4h` which trapped EL0). 210 → 211 tests. Predecessor: P4-Ic4 (`caa49e3` / `81da4eb`).
- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic4 landed — `libthyla-rs` runtime crate extraction.** Lifts `_start` (global_asm!), `#[panic_handler]`, and the SVC wrappers (`t_exits`, `t_puts`, `t_putstr`, `t_mmio_create`, `t_mmio_map`, `t_irq_create`, `t_irq_wait`) + syscall/right/prot constants out of `usr/hello-rs/src/main.rs` into a new `usr/lib/libthyla-rs/` crate (sibling of C-side `usr/lib/libt/`). hello-rs body collapses to ~10 lines. ELF layout pinned identical (66,336-byte binary; `_start` at 0x400000; `rs_main` at 0x400018). Linker keeps `_start` across the rlib boundary via `ENTRY(_start)` in `usr/scripts/aarch64-userspace.ld`. Non-audit-bearing pure Rust refactor. - **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic3 landed — kernel-internal `rfork_with_caps(flags, entry, arg, caps_mask)` capability grant primitive (spec-first).** Closes the v1.0 capability-grant hole that blocked P4-Ic5+: kproc can now spawn a driver Proc holding `CAP_HW_CREATE` via `rfork_with_caps(RFPROC, drv_entry, arg, CAP_HW_CREATE)`. Implementation: `child->caps = __atomic_load_n(&parent->caps, ACQUIRE) & caps_mask` — the AND with the parent's current caps enforces spec invariant `granted ⊆ proc_caps[parent]` regardless of what mask the caller passes. `rfork` becomes a delegate (`return rfork_internal(..., CAP_NONE)`); no churn in existing call sites. Spec-first extension at `specs/handles.tla`: new `proc_ceiling` state var (dynamic per-Proc ceiling — ProcRoot=Caps at Init, child=`proc_caps[parent]` at fork); strengthened `CapsCeiling` to use `proc_ceiling`; new `RforkWithCaps` action; new `BuggyRforkElevate` bug class + `handles_buggy_rfork_elevate.cfg`. **TLC verified across 9 cfgs**: correct cfg 11.7M distinct states clean (8m55s, depth 25); 8 buggy cfgs each produce expected counterexamples. 3 new tests in `kernel/test/test_caps.c`. 207 → 210 tests. ~50 LOC kernel + ~80 LOC spec extension. Predecessor: P4-Ic2 (`39c4de3` / `0e9f1ff`).
- **Earlier tip**: **P4-Ic2 landed — `SYS_MMIO_MAP` syscall + device-memory PTE attrs + demand-page MMIO dispatch + R10 audit closed (1 P1 + 2 P2 + 2 P3 fixed, 1 P3 deferred).** Installs user-VA mappings for KObj_MMIO regions. `mmu_install_user_pte` extended with `bool device_memory` parameter selecting `MAIR_IDX_DEVICE` (nGnRnE) vs `MAIR_IDX_NORMAL_WB`. `userland_demand_page` dispatches on `vma->burrow->type` for PA resolution + device-memory flag. | [43-virtio-gpu.md](reference/43-virtio-gpu.md) | Fourth composed userspace driver (`/virtio-gpu`). | [44-9p-wire.md](reference/44-9p-wire.md) | 9P2000.L wire codec. Pure byte-level marshal/unmarshal; no kernel state, no allocation, no I/O. | [51-pipe.md](reference/51-pipe.md) | Plan 9 `pipe(fd[2])` primitive at the kernel layer. Connected pair of Spoors over a shared 4 KiB ring buffer. | [52-sys-pipe.md](reference/52-sys-pipe.md) | SYS_PIPE = 8 SVC handler. No args; returns rd fd in x0, wr fd in x1. Calls `pipe_create()` + installs both Spoors as KOBJ_SPOOR handles. | [53-sys-rw.md](reference/53-sys-rw.md) | SYS_READ = 9 / SYS_WRITE = 10. fd (x0), buf_va (x1), len (x2). Routes through dev->read/write after rights check + user-VA validation. | [55-sys-attach-9p.md](reference/55-sys-attach-9p.md) | SYS_ATTACH_9P = 13. | [56-sys-mount.md](reference/56-sys-mount.md) | SYS_MOUNT = 14 + SYS_UNMOUNT = 15. Thin wrappers over `kernel/territory.c::mount` / `::unmount`. | [57-attach-probe.md](reference/57-attach-probe.md) | `/attach-probe` userspace integration test of SYS_ATTACH_9P + SYS_MOUNT + SYS_UNMOUNT. | [94-utopia-eval.md](reference/94-utopia-eval.md) | `libutopia::eval` — the rc-shape evaluator for `ut` (U-6 arc). **U-6a + U-6b LANDED**. **U-6b** (statement evaluation): walks `Vec<Statement>` via `eval_statement(env, stmt) -> EvalResult<StatementFlow>` (Normal/Return/Break/Continue) + `eval_block` + `eval_script` + `eval_source` (parse+eval convenience). Implicit-fail (scripture 8.1+8.3+8.9): `eval_block` checks `should_propagate_failure` after each Normal-returning statement (Pipeline's first-element `?`-postfix OR `!env.interactive && implicit_fail_suppressed == 0` AND `$status != 0` → Return). Try/Catch increments `implicit_fail_suppressed`; on body err or post-body `$status != 0`, sets $errstr + $status=1, runs catch. OnNote registers handler in `Env::note_handlers` BTreeMap (runtime delivery wires at U-7). MaskNote pass-through at U-6b. Env extensions: `interactive: bool` (default false; U-6g sets true), `implicit_fail_suppressed: u32`, `trace_depth: u32`, `note_handlers: BTreeMap`. New `eval_word` + `eval_value_token` helpers mirror `eval_expr`'s atom dispatch on Token-shape Word nodes (cross-product Concat for `Word::Concat`). Known v1.x deferral: list literal inside a `for` header (`for (x in (a b c)) { ... }`) parses to UnexpectedEof; the `for (x in $xs)` idiom works (common case). ~620 LOC stmt.rs + ~290 LOC u-test extension; 14 boot probes in `flow_eval_stmt`. **U-6a**: evaluator scaffold + value model + expression evaluation for the no-side-effect subset. Public surface: `Value` (a unified `Vec<String>`; a "scalar" is a one-element list, per scripture §4.1 + §4.2 + §6.3 — uniform representation collapses bash/zsh's scalar-vs-array distinction; argv expansion + `$"var` join + `$#var` length emerge naturally); `Env` (variable scope stack via `Vec<BTreeMap<String, Value>>` with `let_set` writing the topmost frame, bare `assign` walking top-down to the first defining frame else global per scripture §6.2 dynamic scoping; function table; `$status` / `$errstr` / `$cwd` accessors); `EvalError` + `EvalErrorKind` (NonNumeric / DivByZero / Overflow / InvalidShift / NoCaseMatch / NotImplemented / Internal) every error carries a `Span`; `eval_expr(env, expr) -> EvalResult<Value>` recursive walker. Implemented Expr variants: atoms (Word, SingleQuoted, DoubleQuoted with $var + $#var interp; Integer; Var; VarLen; VarNoSplit; VarIndex 1-indexed; VarSlice inclusive); composites (List flattening, Concat with rc-style cross-product); operators (full BinOp arith — Add/Sub/Mul/Div/Mod/Pow/BitAnd/BitOr/BitXor/Shl/Shr — with checked arithmetic; comparison + logical via 0/1 sentinels; numeric-first-else-string comparison rule collapsing scripture §6.13 + §6.14 into one resolution); UnOp (Neg / BitNot / Not); Match (Glob via pattern matcher + In via list membership; Regex returns NotImplemented); Case-as-expression (first-match-wins via glob; NoCaseMatch error if exhausted). Deferred (return NotImplemented at v1.0): Subst/Backtick/ProcSubIn/ProcSubOut (need spawn — U-6f); Match::Regex (need regex engine — v1.x lift). New sibling module `glob` provides the rc/POSIX-shape pattern matcher (`*` no-/ + `?` no-/ + `[abc]` + `[!abc]` + `[a-z]` ranges; bytewise UTF-8-safe). NO filesystem walks — pattern match only, used by case + matches operator; argv-time glob expansion lands at U-6e. ~960 LOC eval (value 165 + env 220 + error 110 + glob 245 + expr 220) + ~480 LOC `#[cfg(test)]` host unit tests + 15 boot-time `flow_eval_expr` probes in /u-test. | [93-utopia-parser.md](reference/93-utopia-parser.md) | `libutopia::parser` stack — the rc-shape parser for `ut` (U-5 arc). **U-5a + U-5b + U-5c + U-5d LANDED; the U-5 arc is COMPLETE**. **U-5a** (tokenizer at `parser/{mod,span,token,error,lexer}.rs`): pure-logic `tokenize(&str) -> Result<Vec<Token>, ParseError>`. Token taxonomy covers bare words (glob meta + `?` disambig), single + double-quoted strings (with `DqPart` parts), top-level `$var` / `$#var` / `$"var` / `$(cmd)` / `` `{cmd}` ``, process substitution `<(cmd)` / `>(cmd)`, heredocs with FIFO body collection, regex literal after `=~` (one-shot), all operators + 16 reserved words. Every token carries `Span { start, end }`. **U-5b** (parser core + AST at `parser/{ast,parse}.rs`): recursive-descent `parse(&str) -> Result<Script, ParseError>` + `parse_tokens(Vec<Token>, source_len)`. AST covers Script + Statement (Pipeline / If / For / While / FnDecl / Let / Assign / Return / Break / Continue), Pipeline + PipelineElement (with `?|` -> `tolerate_failure` on LEFT element + trailing `&` -> `background`), Command (Simple / BraceBlock / Subshell / Arith), Word (Single or span-adjacent `^`-joined Concat), Redirect (Stdin / Stdout / Append / Heredoc-with-inline-body via parser's FIFO pre-extracted body queue). Locked design decisions: strict rc (`--key=value` -> `UnexpectedEqualInCommand`); `^` requires span-adjacency on both sides; postfix `?` requires statement terminator; `case` / `try` / `trace` / `on` / `mask` deferred to U-5d. Single-error-stop semantics. **U-5c** (expression parser at `parser/expr.rs`): `parse_expr_tokens(Vec<Token>, source_len, ExprContext) -> Result<Expr, ParseError>`. Pratt-style precedence climbing for arith; eagerly parsed substitution bodies (`$()`, `` `{} `` lift to sub-Scripts); full operator surface for Cond context (match/compare/logical); upfront arith retokenization that splits Word tokens containing operator chars (`+ - * /`) into proper Plus/Minus/Star/Slash tokens. The AST now has ONE canonical shape: `IfStmt.cond` / `ForStmt.list_expr` / `WhileStmt.cond` / `LetStmt.value` / `AssignStmt.value` / `Return(Option<Expr>)` / `CommandKind::Arith(Expr)` all hold `Expr` (was `Vec<Token>` at U-5b). New `ExprKind` variants cover Atoms (Word/SingleQuoted/DoubleQuoted/Integer/Var/VarLen/VarNoSplit/VarIndex/VarSlice/Subst/Backtick/ProcSubIn/ProcSubOut/Regex), Composites (List/Concat), Operators (BinOp/UnOp/Match). New error kinds: `EmptyExpression`, `UnexpectedTokenInExpr`, `InvalidArithLiteral`, `InvalidVarIndex`, `TrailingTokensInExpr`. **U-5d** (pattern matching + try/catch + trace + on/mask + case-as-expression at `parser/{parse,expr,ast,error}.rs`): five new `StatementKind` variants (`Case` / `Try` / `Trace` / `OnNote` / `MaskNote`) + one new `ExprKind` variant (`Case`) for case-as-expression in any context. Each case arm has a Statement body (statement form) or Expr value (expression form); patterns are space-separated value-position Exprs (`*` is just `Word("*")`); `catch` required after `try`; `on note 'name' { ... }` matches the literal `Word("note")` (note is NOT a reserved keyword); note names accept any Value-context Expr. Pattern collection reuses `split_value_tokens_on_whitespace` (formerly `split_index_body`, now `pub(super)`). New `ParseErrorKind::EmptyCasePattern`. ~900 LOC lexer + ~1400 LOC parser + ~450 LOC AST + ~1350 LOC expr + ~2100 LOC `#[cfg(test)]` tests (145 total) + 37 boot-time probes (7 lexer + 8 parser-core + 10 parser-expr + 12 parser-full). The U-5 parser arc is COMPLETE; the parser's public surface is ready for U-6's evaluator. | medium | **U-5 arc COMPLETE** |
| [92-utopia-line-editor.md](reference/92-utopia-line-editor.md) | `libutopia::line_editor` engine (U-4 arc complete: U-4a + U-4b + U-4c + U-4d) — line editor sub-arc of Phase 7. **U-4a** (engine core): `LineEditor` + `EditorAction` (NoChange / Redraw / Accept / Cancel / Eof / ClearScreen) + ANSI input parser state machine (Ground / Escape / Csi / Utf8) + emacs editing primitives + UTF-8 multi-byte accumulation + single-line `render(prompt)` + new `libutopia::ansi::visible_width` helper. UTF-8 boundary-safe; 64 KiB buffer cap. **U-4b** (multi-line + bracket-balance): `BalanceState` + `balance(s)` lightweight tracker (brace/paren/bracket depth, single + double quotes, escape, `#` comments, trailing unescaped backslash). Enter inserts `\n` instead of Accept when unbalanced; trailing `\` stays in buffer (parser elides `\\\n`). Multi-line `render(prompt)` emits prompt + `⋮` continuation prefix per UTOPIA-VISUAL.md §3.2 with `\x1b[<n>F` cursor up-positioning. Backspace + Delete auto-join lines. **U-4c** (history nav + Ctrl-R search): smart Up/Down (multi-line cursor nav when not on first/last line; history-prev/next otherwise; column-preserving via `desired_col` sticky tracker); Ctrl-R incremental search (substring match; Ctrl-R steps back to next-older match, Ctrl-N forward, Enter Accepts, Ctrl-C / Ctrl-G cancels + restores saved buffer/cursor; readline-style `(reverse-i-search)\`<query>': <matched_line>` render); history cap of 10000 entries (FIFO eviction); new public accessors `is_searching` / `search_query` / `search_match_index`. NO raw-mode I/O (deferred to U-6 + U-PTY). Tab no-op (U-4d). **U-4d** (Tab completion): new `CompletionSource` trait + `Completions { replace_range, candidates }` struct + shipped `StaticCompletionSource` (word-prefix matcher; preserves source order) + `longest_common_prefix` UTF-8-safe helper. New `LineEditor::set_completion_source` / `clear_completion_source` (Box<dyn>). New `EditorAction::ShowCompletions(Vec<String>)` variant emitted when 2+ candidates have no further common-prefix extension. Tab key now maps to `Action::Complete` (was `Action::Ignore` at U-4a). Dispatch: 0 candidates → NoChange; 1 candidate → replace + Redraw; 2+ candidates with extending common-prefix → extend (Redraw); 2+ with no extension → ShowCompletions. ~1620 LOC engine + ~760 LOC `#[cfg(test)]` host unit tests + 16 boot-time `flow_line_editor` probes in /u-test (6 U-4a + 4 U-4b + 3 U-4c + 3 U-4d). New joey line: `u-test: line editor OK`. | medium | **U-4 arc complete (a+b+c+d landed)** |
| [91-utopia.md](reference/91-utopia.md) | `usr/utopia/` workspace skeleton + `ut` shell skeleton (U-3) — the **first chunk in the shell half of Phase 7**. New `libutopia` crate (palette + ansi + path modules) and `utopia-shell` crate (the `ut` binary, v0.0.1-skeleton: Pale Fire version banner + clean exit). Workspace placement: `utopia/libutopia` + `utopia/shell` added as members of the existing `usr/Cargo.toml` (small deviation from UTOPIA-SHELL-DESIGN.md section 14.1's "Cargo workspace root at usr/utopia/" sketch — directory grouping preserved, single Cargo workspace; lift to a separate workspace is mechanical if needed). `tools/build.sh::build_userspace` builds the new crates via the existing cargo invocation; cpio extended with `ut`; joey spawns `/ut` after `/u-test` and verifies status=0. Banner emits 24-bit-colour SGR escapes (glyph ember orange `#e07840` + path receded steel `#8898b4`) per UTOPIA-VISUAL.md; verified end-to-end via the boot log. Skeleton scope -- no REPL, no line editor, no parser, no evaluator at U-3; U-4..U-Z arc fills those in. | medium | **U-3 landed** |
| [89-hardware.md](reference/89-hardware.md) | `libthyla_rs::hardware::{Mmio, Irq, Dma}` — typed RAII wrappers over the kernel `KObj_MMIO` / `KObj_IRQ` / `KObj_DMA` surfaces (U-2h-hardware). Combined create + map constructors; Drop closes the handle (the kernel-side Burrow keeps the mapping alive until proc exit). Type-system-enforced non-transferability per I-5 (no `Transfer` trait impl). Volatile MMIO `read_u32` / `write_u32` with runtime bounds + alignment asserts. DMA buffers are normal memory with `as_slice` / `as_slice_mut` views + 32-bit accessors with compiler fences; hardware barriers remain the caller's responsibility. Irq impls `t::poll::AsFd` for `PollSet` composition. Bare SVC wrappers (`t_mmio_create` etc.) remain exported. Migrated consumers: mmio-probe, irq-probe, irq-bench (3 simple probes; the positive paths through real PL031 RTC + GIC SPI 96). 7 virtio-* binaries continue to use bare wrappers; migration is mechanical and can land incrementally. | small | **U-2h-hardware landed** |
| [85-pouch-stratumd-build.md](reference/85-pouch-stratumd-build.md) | stratumd cross-compiled against the pouch sysroot for `aarch64-thylacine` (P6-pouch-stratumd-build sub-chunk 15) — the first non-trivial daemon ported via pouch. `tools/build.sh::build_stratumd` drives Stratum's CMake tree (consumed from `$STRATUM_SRC` defaulting to `~/projects/stratum/v2`) through the pouch toolchain; configure-flags disable Linux-only features (io_uring / libaio / liboqs PQ) + tests + fuzzers + Werror. | [73-sys-spawn-with-perms.md](reference/73-sys-spawn-with-perms.md) | `SYS_SPAWN_WITH_PERMS = 31` (P5-corvus-srv-impl-b3a) — race-free spawn-time stamp of `PROC_FLAG_*` bits. Extends `SYS_SPAWN_FULL` with a sixth `perm_flags` arg the kernel stamps on the child atomically inside the spawn thunk BEFORE `exec_setup`. **`SPAWN_PERM_MAY_POST_SERVICE`** is the v1.0 bit; gated on the calling Proc being `CONSOLE_ATTACHED`. Closes the race window a post-spawn `mark(child_pid)` syscall would open. The joey-stamp mechanism for `PROC_FLAG_MAY_POST_SERVICE` (corvus's post-gate). 4 new tests (`sys_spawn_with_perms.*`). | small | **P5-corvus-srv-impl-b3a landed** |
| [72-poll.md](reference/72-poll.md) | The multi-fd wait/wake primitive (P5-poll-a) — `struct pollfd` + the `Dev.poll` vtable slot + `kernel/poll.c` + `SYS_POLL` (syscall 29) + `devpipe`'s real `.poll`. The poller sleeps on its OWN private `Rendez` via `tsleep` (preserving single-waiter discipline) and installs a `poll_waiter` hook on each polled object's hook list; register-then-observe is load-bearing. Lock order object → list → rendez. Spec: `specs/poll.tla`'s `Register` / `CommitOrSleep` / `MakeReady` / `NoStaleHook`. `devsrv` poll lands at P5-poll-b. | medium | **P5-poll-a landed** |
| [71-srvconn.md](reference/71-srvconn.md) | The `/srv` per-connection transport (P5-corvus-srv-impl-a3a) — a `SrvConn` is one kernel-minted `/srv` connection: a bidirectional `tsleep`-bounded byte transport (two rings, `c2s` + `s2c`) plus the opening client Proc's kernel-stamped peer identity (`stripes`, console bit, pid) captured by value, and a dedicated synchronous kernel `p9_client` (kernel-owned, never in a handle table — C-23). The connection layer the `/srv` registry (reference 70) mediates per client; the `devsrv` walk/open path that mints a `SrvConn`, the accept queue, and `SYS_SRV_ACCEPT` are -impl-a3b. No new spec — transport plumbing over `specs/tsleep.tla` / `specs/pipe.tla`. | medium | **P5-corvus-srv-impl-a3a landed** |
| [70-devsrv.md](reference/70-devsrv.md) | The `/srv` service registry (P5-corvus-srv-impl-a2) — the `devsrv` kernel Dev (Plan 9 `#s`), the service registry, `SYS_POST_SERVICE`, the joey-stamped `PROC_FLAG_MAY_POST_SERVICE` post-gate, and poster-exit tombstoning. The kernel surface a userspace 9P server (`corvus`) posts itself on; the per-connection layer is -impl-a3. | [69-corvus-unwrap.md](reference/69-corvus-unwrap.md) | corvus WRAP/UNWRAP + the ML-KEM-768 + X25519 hybrid keypair (P5-corvus-bringup-d) — the real hybrid keypair, the hybrid-PKE DEK envelope, and the C-7-gated WRAP (verb 10) + UNWRAP (verb 4) verbs. |
| [68-corvus-crypto.md](reference/68-corvus-crypto.md) | corvus real crypto (P5-corvus-bringup-c) — Argon2id passphrase verification + AEGIS-256 AEAD + the `CRVS` state-file format + the USER_CREATE verb. Pure-Rust `argon2` / `aegis` (`pure-rust` feature) / `linked_list_allocator` crates; a 24 MiB static-BSS `#[global_allocator]` heap. AUTH now verifies the passphrase via an Argon2id-derived KEK + AEGIS-256-unwrap of a wrapped keypair (placeholder; ML-KEM-768+X25519 hybrid deferred). State records in-memory at this sub-chunk. Argon2id `m_cost=16 MiB` (capped below the design's 64 MiB default for the contiguous heap). | medium | **P5-corvus-bringup-c landed** |
| [67-el1h-kernel.md](reference/67-el1h-kernel.md) | Uniform-EL1h kernel execution model (P5-el1h-kernel) — the kernel runs entirely at EL1h (`SPSel=1`, `sp=SP_EL1`=the running thread's own kernel stack; `SP_EL0` exclusively the userspace stack — invariant I-21). Records the conversion that fixed a pre-existing SMP soundness bug: the former EL1t/EL1h dual-mode kernel let a work-stolen thread resume `KERNEL_EXIT` at the wrong mode, where `msr SP_EL0` traps `EC=0` and silently killed a secondary CPU on every boot. Exception frames now build on the per-thread kernel stack (migration-safe). `start.S`/`vectors.S`/`userland.S` converted; `cpu_switch_context` unchanged. Pinned by `specs/sched_ctxsw.tla`. | medium | **P5-el1h-kernel landed** |
| [66-corvus-server.md](reference/66-corvus-server.md) | `/sbin/corvus` server loop + binary frame wire codec (P5-corvus-bringup-b) — second impl chunk of the corvus daemon. Extends -a's skeleton to a single-peer Spoor server reading framed verb requests on fd 0, writing responses on fd 1, exits 0 on rx EOF. Wire format per CORVUS-DESIGN.md §6.4: req=verb_id+payload_len+payload, resp=status+payload_len+payload. Two verbs land: **AUTH** (parses user+passphrase; passphrase NOT verified at this skeleton — Argon2id at -c; mints 33-byte session token = `'s'` + 32 hex chars of CSPRNG entropy) + **SESSION_CLOSE** (clears session by token). Single-slot session table; `Session::user` is set once at install + never mutated until clear (structural C-3 enforcement). Joey extended to drive AUTH + SESSION_CLOSE round-trip via `t_spawn_full` with pipe-pair + caps. Spec actions `AuthSuccess` + `SessionClose` wired through. libthyla-rs gained `t_pipe` / `t_read` / `t_write` / `t_close` Rust wrappers. | medium | **P5-corvus-bringup-b landed** |
| [65-corvus-skeleton.md](reference/65-corvus-skeleton.md) | `/sbin/corvus` skeleton (P5-corvus-bringup-a) — first impl chunk of the Thylacine-native key-agent daemon. `usr/corvus/` Rust crate runs the 5 v1.0 hardening syscalls (mlockall + set_dumpable + set_traceable + getrandom-seeded probe + explicit_bzero) and exits 0. Production-shape orchestration: joey spawns /sbin/corvus via `SYS_SPAWN_WITH_CAPS` with `CAP_LOCK_PAGES \| CAP_CSPRNG_READ`. Joey's own caps bumped to `CAP_ALL` via `rfork_with_caps` at boot so it can delegate. Pins CORVUS-DESIGN.md C-2 + C-5 (RAM-wipe pattern) + C-15 (CSPRNG-seeded probe) at the runtime layer; C-3 / C-7 / C-11 (session machine + verb dispatch) deferred to P5-corvus-bringup-b onward. Boot path is the regression — `corvus: ready` + joey reaps status=0 = test passes. | small | **P5-corvus-bringup-a landed** |
| [64-sys-spawn-full.md](reference/64-sys-spawn-full.md) | `SYS_SPAWN_FULL` = 25 — fourth spawn variant combining fd inheritance + cap-subset in one call. Needed at P5-corvus-bringup. 5 new tests; cap inspection race-free, fd inheritance verified indirectly via clean-exit + existing /stub-driver coverage. | small | **P5-spawn-full landed** |
| [48-dev9p.md](reference/48-dev9p.md) | Dev vtable proxying to the kernel 9P client. The foundation of ARCH §9.6 "filesystem-as-Spoor" — makes a p9_client-backed Spoor look identical to a kernel-internal Dev above the Spoor walk algorithm. Per-Spoor state: `struct dev9p_priv { magic, client *, fid, fid_owned }`. Root Spoors don't own root_fid (higher layer manages); walk-derived Spoors do (close clunks). Public constructor: `dev9p_attach_client(client, root_fid) → Spoor *`. No spec extension (pure composition over spec'd lower layers). | medium | **P5-attach-dev landed** |
| [47-9p-client.md](reference/47-9p-client.md) | 9P client high-level API: 25 op wrappers (lifecycle, handshake, walk, clunk, IO, metadata, mutation) consolidating wire + session + transport into one callable surface. Every op: `session.send → transport.exchange → result extraction → error mapping`. Signed-errno convention (0 / -EINVAL / -EBUSY / -EIO / -ecode). Caller-allocated `struct p9_client` (~12 KiB, embeds session + transport + outbound buffer). Internal field-by-field copy helpers replace implicit memcpy struct assignments (kernel doesn't link libc). No spec extension needed (pure composition). | medium | **P5-client landed** |

---

## Document maintenance

When a chunk lands (bug fix, refactor, new module), the author is responsible for:

1. Updating the relevant `reference/NN-*.md` section(s).
2. Refreshing the [Snapshot](#snapshot) figures.
3. If the chunk introduces or refutes an invariant, updating the spec catalog entry.
4. If a new term or acronym enters the lexicon, updating the glossary.

Reference sections are PR-first like any code change; the audit policy in `CLAUDE.md` extends here: a change to a documented invariant updates the spec FIRST, then the reference, then the code. If the three disagree, the spec wins.

---

## Glossary

See `ARCHITECTURE.md §29` for the definitive glossary. As implementation lands and new terms enter the lexicon, they're appended to that glossary; this reference points to it rather than duplicating.

PAC/MMU/VBAR/TPIDR all set per-CPU. Cross-CPU PAC consistency (shared g_pac_keys) ready for P2-Ce thread migration. Per-CPU run trees + idle thread integration deferred to P2-Cd. |
| 2026-05-06 | **P2-Ga landed.** ELF64 ARM64 loader (parse + W^X validation). New `kernel/include/thylacine/elf.h` (~210 LOC) defines `Elf64_Ehdr` (64 B; pinned via `_Static_assert`) + `Elf64_Phdr` (56 B; pinned) + ELF magic/class/data/version/OSABI/machine/type constants + program header types (PT_LOAD/PT_INTERP/PT_GNU_STACK/etc.) + flag bits (PF_R/W/X) + `elf_load_result` error enum (21 distinct codes) + `elf_image` output struct. New `kernel/elf.c` (~150 LOC) implements `elf_load(blob, size, *out)` as a 5-stage validation pipeline: (1) e_ident, (2) e_type/e_machine/e_version, (3) phdr table layout with overflow-safe phoff + phnum*phentsize, (4) per-segment validation with W^X rejection at the loader layer (mask off PF_MASKOS/PF_MASKPROC bits; check architectural PF_W & PF_X for both-set; reject), (5) entry-in-segment validation. Each additive arithmetic uses overflow-safe helpers (`u64_add_overflow`, widening u32*u32). Per-segment flags stripped to architectural PF_R/W/X bits before storing in elf_load_segment. Phase tag P2-Fd → P2-Ga. New reference doc `docs/reference/21-elf.md` covers full API + impl + test mapping + caveats. New 6 in-kernel tests in `kernel/test/test_elf.c`: parse_minimal_ok, parse_multi_segment_ok (text RX + rodata R + data RW), header_rejection (exhaustive matrix: magic/class/data/ident-version/OSABI/type ET_REL+ET_DYN/machine non-AArch64/file-version/phentsize), rwx_rejected (PF_R+PF_W+PF_X and PF_W+PF_X both rejected; RX/RW + OS-specific bits accepted), bounds_rejection (TOO_SMALL/NULL/no-phdrs/too-many-phdrs/phtab-OOB/filesz>memsz/seg-OOB), policy_rejection (PT_INTERP/PT_GNU_STACK-with-PF_X/entry==0/entry-outside-segment + final positive control). Skipped TLA+ spec per CLAUDE.md "ELF parsing is config parsing" guidance. ARCH §28 I-12 enforced at the third (loader) layer; PTE bit + mprotect are the other two. Static ET_EXEC at v1.0 (PT_INTERP/ET_DYN/PIE/PT_DYNAMIC/PT_TLS deferred to Phase 5+ dynamic-linker support). | 2026-05-06 | **P2-Fd landed.** Kernel BURROW impl. New `kernel/include/thylacine/burrow.h` defines `enum burrow_type` (BURROW_TYPE_ANON at v1.0; PHYS at Phase 3; FILE post-v1.0); `struct Burrow` (~50 B; magic at offset 0 for SLUB freelist clobber UAF defense; size + page_count + handle_count + mapping_count + pages chunk + order). New `kernel/burrow.c` (~190 LOC) implements `burrow_init` (SLUB cache), `burrow_create_anon(size)` (eager allocation via alloc_pages(order, KP_ZERO) where order = ceil_log2(page_count); rounds up wastes some pages but simple), `burrow_ref` / `burrow_unref` (handle_count++/--), `burrow_map` / `burrow_unmap` (mapping_count++/--; refcount-only at v1.0 — Phase 3 wires actual VMA), `burrow_get_size` / `burrow_handle_count` / `burrow_mapping_count` (read-only accessors), cumulative diagnostic counters. The dual-check `if (handle_count == 0 && mapping_count == 0) burrow_free_internal(v)` at the END of both `burrow_unref` AND `burrow_unmap` is the runtime enforcement of `specs/burrow.tla::NoUseAfterFree` — neither premature free (counts > 0 ∧ pages dead) nor delayed free (counts = 0 ∧ pages alive) is reachable. `kernel/handle.c` extended with `handle_release_obj(kind, obj)` + `handle_acquire_obj(kind, obj)` per-kind dispatchers; KOBJ_BURROW calls burrow_ref / burrow_unref. `handle_close`, `handle_dup`, and `handle_table_free` all call through to maintain refcounts correctly. `handle_dup` rolls back the acquire on alloc failure. `kernel/main.c` bootstrap order: territory_init → handle_init → **burrow_init** → proc_init → thread_init. New reference doc `docs/reference/20-burrow.md` covers full API + impl + spec mapping + caveats. New 6 in-kernel tests in `kernel/test/test_burrow.c`: `create_close_round_trip` (basic + counters), `refcount_lifecycle` (multi-handle ref/unref), `map_unmap_lifecycle` (handle_count → 0 with mapping_count > 0 must NOT free), `handles_x_mappings_matrix` (6 cross-product cases verifying NoUseAfterFree at every boundary), `via_handle_table` (end-to-end through handle_alloc/dup/close), `handle_table_orphan_cleanup` (proc_free with open BURROW handles releases refs correctly). | 2026-05-06 | **P2-Eb landed.** Kernel territory impl. New `kernel/include/thylacine/territory.h` defines `struct Territory { u64 magic; int ref; int nbinds; struct PgrpBind binds[PGRP_MAX_BINDS=8] }` (80 bytes; magic at offset 0 for double-free defense). New `kernel/territory.c` (~150 LOC) implements `territory_init` (boot-time SLUB cache + kpgrp allocation), `territory_alloc` / `territory_clone` / `territory_ref` / `territory_unref`, `bind` / `unmount`. `bind`'s `would_create_cycle` precondition is a fixed-point reachability iteration over the existing edges; rejects with -1 if adding `dst -> src` would close a cycle (matches spec's `WouldCreateCycle` exactly). `struct Proc` grew 80→88 bytes with the `struct Territory *territory` field; `_Static_assert` updated. `proc_init` now requires `territory_init` to have run (kproc gets kpgrp at allocation). `rfork(RFPROC)` calls `territory_clone(parent->territory)` for the child's territory; OOM rolls back the proc allocation. `proc_free` calls `territory_unref(p->territory)` before slab release. `main.c` bootstrap order: slub_init → territory_init → proc_init → thread_init. PGRP_MAX_BINDS = 8 chosen to keep the Territory struct under 80 bytes — SLUB's KP_ZERO byte-loop on a larger struct (e.g., 32 entries = 272 bytes) inflated the proc.rfork_stress_1000 boot time past the 500 ms VISION §4 budget under QEMU emulation. New reference doc `docs/reference/18-territory.md` covers API + impl + spec mapping + caveats. New 3 in-kernel tests in `kernel/test/test_territory.c`: `bind_smoke` (round-trip + idempotency + unmount), `cycle_rejected` (spec NoCycle invariant verification: 3-node chain rejects cycle-closing bind + self-bind), `fork_isolated` (territory_clone deep-copy verification: parent and child evolve independently). | 2026-05-06 | **P2-Ea landed.** New spec `specs/territory.tla` (~165 LOC TLA+) + `territory.cfg` + `namespace_buggy.cfg`. Models Plan 9 `bind` as a directed graph: edge `dst → src` means walking `dst` produces `src` (per ARCH §9.1). Cycle-freedom (ARCH §28 I-3) is the primary state invariant: `NoCycle == ∀ p ∈ Procs, x ∈ Paths : x ∉ Reachable(p, bindings[p][x])`. The `Bind` action's precondition is `~WouldCreateCycle(p, src, dst)` — adding the edge `dst → src` is rejected if `dst` is already reachable from `src` (which would close the loop `src → ... → dst → src`). `BuggyBind` skips the cycle check; counterexample at depth 4 / 95 states. Isolation (ARCH §28 I-1) is structural in the data model: bindings[p] and bindings[q] for p#q are independent function values; no action updates two procs simultaneously. RFNAMEG sharing deliberately deferred until Phase 5+ syscall surface lands (impl extincts on non-RFPROC at v1.0). `ForkClone(parent, child)` action models rfork(RFPROC)'s territory copy; `Unbind` mirrors `unmount`. `specs/SPEC-TO-CODE.md` updated with the territory.tla mapping pointing at P2-Eb impl targets (`kernel/territory.c::bind`, etc.). Phase tag P2-Dc → P2-Ea. P2-Eb (kernel/territory.c impl) is the next sub-chunk. | 25/25 tests; 4/4 fault matrix; ~265 ms boot (production); ~312 ms UBSan; KASLR 5/5 distinct; **scheduler.tla TLC-clean (10188 states); territory.tla TLC-clean (625 states); namespace_buggy.cfg counterexample at depth 4 / 95 states**. |
| 2026-05-06 | **P2-Dc landed.** Per-thread kstack guard pages. Closes P2-A trip-hazard #1 (kstack overflow detection). thread_create now allocates 8 pages (32 KiB at order=3) instead of 4; upper 4 pages = 16 KiB usable kstack, lower 4 pages = 16 KiB no-access guard. New `THREAD_KSTACK_TOTAL_SIZE` / `THREAD_KSTACK_TOTAL_ORDER` / `THREAD_KSTACK_GUARD_SIZE` / `THREAD_KSTACK_GUARD_PAGES` constants in `<thylacine/thread.h>`. New MMU API in `arch/arm64/mmu.{h,c}`: `mmu_set_no_access(pa)` + `mmu_restore_normal(pa)` (single-page) and `mmu_set_no_access_range(pa, n)` + `mmu_restore_normal_range(pa, n)` (batched, single TLB flush — substantially faster at thread_create / thread_free volume). The L2 block descriptor covering the kstack PA is demoted to an L3 table on first guard insertion: a fresh page from buddy is initialized with 512 × PTE_KERN_RW page descriptors reproducing the original block's mapping, then the L2 entry is break-before-make replaced with a table pointer. Subsequent guards in the same 2 MiB block reuse the existing L3. The exception handler's `addr_is_stack_guard()` now also checks the current thread's kstack guard region (in addition to the boot-stack guard from start.S) — overflow into a guard page produces "EXTINCTION: kernel stack overflow" with FAR pointing into the guard. New `THYLACINE_FAULT_TEST=kstack_overflow` variant in `kernel/fault_test.c`: spawns a thread that recursively allocates 1 KiB stack frames; ~16 frames overflow the 16 KiB usable region into the guard. `tools/test-fault.sh kstack_overflow` PASSes on observing the extinction. `addr_is_stack_guard()` exception path now `#include`s `<thylacine/thread.h>` for `current_thread()` access. SMP-safety note: thread_create/thread_free are single-CPU at v1.0; concurrent demote at Phase 5+ requires a global mmu_lock. test_context.c bumped to expect THREAD_KSTACK_TOTAL_SIZE (32 KiB). Phase tag P2-Db → P2-Dc. | 25/25 tests; 4/4 fault matrix (canary, W^X, BTI, **kstack_overflow** new); ~236 ms boot (production); ~285 ms (UBSan); KASLR 5/5 distinct; scheduler.tla TLC-clean (10188 states). |
| 2026-05-06 | **P2-Db landed.** Lifecycle stress upgraded to 1000 iterations in batches of 8 (`proc.rfork_stress_100` → `proc.rfork_stress_1000`). Each batch fans out 8 children before reaping any — exercises the run tree's depth + the wait_pid Rendez under sustained load. Per-CPU run counters track which CPU executed each child; sum-must-equal-ITERS check verifies no double-reap or missed run. Cross-CPU placement assertion lifted out: at this phase secondaries don't run their own timer IRQs (per-CPU timer init lands later) and rfork doesn't yet send IPI_RESCHED to peers, so children placed by ready() in the local run tree are typically picked by the same CPU before secondaries can steal — a dedicated cross-CPU test lands once either secondary timers OR rfork-driven IPI_RESCHED is wired (P2-Dd or post-P2-Db). Per-thread guard pages (kstack underflow detection — closes P2-A trip-hazard #1) deferred to P2-Dc: requires L2-block → L3-table demotion in `arch/arm64/mmu.c` because kstacks live in 2 MiB-block-mapped RAM, and per-page no-access protection requires 4 KiB granularity. | 2026-05-05 | **P2-Da landed.** rfork(RFPROC, entry, arg) + exits(msg) + wait_pid(*status). struct Proc grew 24→80 bytes with state + parent/children/sibling + exit_status + exit_msg + child_done Rendez. exits() transitions Proc to ZOMBIE, marks calling Thread EXITING, wakes parent's child_done; sched() leaves EXITING out of run tree. wait_pid() blocks on parent's child_done Rendez until any child is ZOMBIE; reaps via thread_free + proc_free.
